Limits of Insurance Provisions

CG 00 01 policy form Policy No. GL695378

Item CGL-0008 Class / Territory 47103 / 003 Exposure Payroll 171,494 Limit General Aggregate: $2,000,000 Premium $8,831 Form CG 00 01 09 21

The amounts shown in the declarations for Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, represent the maximum sums we will disburse, regardless of the number of insureds, claims made, or persons or organizations bringing suit. The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence. The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000. The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000. The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000. Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy. References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule. Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations. If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date. The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries. Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy. A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Commercial General Liability Conditions

CG 00 01 policy form Policy No. GL695378

Item CGL-0009 Class / Territory 10010 / 007 Exposure Gross sales 187,369 Limit Products-Completed Operations Aggregate: $2,000,000 Premium $13,940 Form CG 20 10 04 13

This section outlines the responsibilities of both the insured and the insurer under this policy. Compliance with these conditions is essential for the proper administration of coverage. In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses. The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured. No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage. If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement. We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This is to ensure accurate premium determination. References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 10010 at Location 3 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule. Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations. If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date. The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries. Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy. A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Who Is An Insured

CG 00 01 policy form Policy No. GL695378

Item CGL-0010 Class / Territory 41670 / 007 Exposure Gross sales 200,180 Limit Personal and Advertising Injury: $1,000,000 Premium $14,893 Form CG 20 37 09 21

The named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, as shown in the declarations, is an insured. This includes any individual partners, members, or their spouses, but only with respect to the conduct of your business. If the named insured is a limited liability company, its members are insureds, but only with respect to the conduct of your business. Its managers are also insureds, but only with respect to their duties as your managers. Any executive officer or director of the named insured is an insured, but only with respect to their duties as an officer or director. Stockholders are also insureds, but only with respect to their liability as stockholders. Any person or organization acting as your real estate manager is an insured. This applies only with respect to their duties as your real estate manager. Any person or organization having temporary custody of your property if you die is an insured, but only with respect to liability arising out of the maintenance or use of that property. Any newly acquired or formed organization, other than a partnership, joint venture, or limited liability company, over which you maintain ownership or majority interest, will be an insured for up to 90 days or until the end of the policy period, whichever is earlier. References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 41670 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule. Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations. Item CGL-0011 Class / Territory 16916 / 007 Exposure Cost of work 222,062 Limit Damage to Premises Rented to You: $100,000 Premium $2,487 Form CG 21 06 04 13

This coverage part outlines the protection provided for certain liabilities arising from your business operations. It applies to bodily injury and property damage occurring during the policy period, as further detailed in the declarations. We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage. The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage. This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage. The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part. References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 16916 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule. Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations. If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date. The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries. Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy. A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued. Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.
